    <script src="/build/prebid-ads-advertisement_adbanner.6dee89ae.js" type="text/javascript"></script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    analyticsEvent = function () {
    };
    analyticsVPV = function () {
    };
    analyticsClearVPV = function () {
    };
    analyticsForm = function () {
    };

    var googleTrackingParameters = {"page":{"type":"frontpages"},"content":{"title":"\/","paymentModel":"free"},"event":"dataLayerPush"};
    var googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts = [];
    var requiredDataLayerPartsMemento = [...googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts];

    function setArticleStats() {
        $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {
                has_audio: 0,
                number_of_links: 0,
                number_of_embeds: 0,
            }});
    }

    function setPageType() {
        var pageType = window.dfpConfig && window.dfpConfig.targetingParams && window.dfpConfig.targetingParams.articleType;

        if (pageType) {
            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {page: {type: pageType}});
        }
    }

    var isDataLayerReady = false;
    function setDataLayer() {
        if (googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts.length === 0) {
            if (googleTrackingParameters.user && googleTrackingParameters.user.access === undefined) {
                googleTrackingParameters.user.access = 1;
            }

            window.dataLayer.push(googleTrackingParameters);

            if(!isDataLayerReady) {
                isDataLayerReady = true;
                document.dispatchEvent(new Event('DataLayerReady'));
            }
        }
    }

    function setUserData() {
        try {
            var userInfoData = $.parseJSON(window.Cookies.get("userInfo") || "{}");

            var reqrole = 'Anonymous';
            if (userInfoData.roles !== undefined) {
                reqrole = userInfoData.roles.join(',');
            }

            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {user: mapUserData(userInfoData)});
            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {reqrole: reqrole}});

        } catch (e) {
            console.error("GTM tracking issue", e);
        }
        removeElementFromArray('UserInfoData', googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts);
    }

    function mapUserData($userInfoData) {
        var userData = {
            'gigyaID': (($userInfoData.userId !== undefined) && ($userInfoData.userId !== null)) ? $userInfoData.userId : null,
            'auth': (($userInfoData.userId !== undefined) && ($userInfoData.userId !== null)) ? 1 : 0,
            'uid': $userInfoData.UID
        };

        if ($userInfoData.subscriptionType !== undefined && $userInfoData.subscriptionType !== null) {
            userData.subscriptionType = $userInfoData.subscriptionType;
        }

        return userData;
    }

    function removeElementFromArray(value, array) {
        index = array.indexOf(value);
        if (index != -1) {
            array.splice(index, 1);
        }
    }

    function setAdblockData() {
        if (typeof adblockJsFile === 'undefined') {
            adblockJsFile = 0;
        }
        $.extend(googleTrackingParameters, {
            adblock: !adblockJsFile
        });
        removeElementFromArray('AdblockData', googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts);
    }

    function setPaywallData(event) {
        var $paywallData = event.detail;

        $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {user: {access: $paywallData.access ? 1 : 0}});

        if ($paywallData.type) {
            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {paywall: $paywallData.type}});
        }
        if ($paywallData.paymentModel) {
            $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {paymentModel: $paywallData.paymentModel}});
        }

        removeElementFromArray('PaywallData', googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts);
        setDataLayer();
    }

    function setLoginWallData(event) {
      var loginWallData = event.detail;

      if (!loginWallData.visible) {
        $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {user: {access: 1}});
        $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {loginwall: null}});
        if (!loginWallData.enabled) {
          removeElementFromArray('LoginWallData', requiredDataLayerPartsMemento)
        }
        fulfillLoginWallData();

        return;
      }

      $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {content: {loginwall: loginWallData.type + '-' + loginWallData.option}});
      if ('hard' === loginWallData.type) {
        $.extend(true, googleTrackingParameters, {user: {access: 0}});
      }

      fulfillLoginWallData();
    }

    function fulfillLoginWallData() {
      removeElementFromArray('LoginWallData', googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts);
      setDataLayer();
    }

    function initializeDataLayer(initial) {
        if (!initial) {
            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
        }
        setArticleStats();
        setPageType();
        setUserData();
        setDataLayer();
        setAdblockData();
    }

    initializeDataLayer(true);

    var onDataLayerReady = function (callback) {
        if (isDataLayerReady) {
            callback();
        } else {
            document.addEventListener("DataLayerReady", callback);
        }
    }

    document.addEventListener('PaywallInitialized', setPaywallData);
    $(document).on('loginSuccess logout', function () {
        if (requiredDataLayerPartsMemento.includes('LoginWallData') && !googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts.includes('LoginWallData')) {
            googleTrackingRequiredDataLayerParts.push('LoginWallData');
        }
        initializeDataLayer(false);
    });
    window.addEventListener('LoginWallInitialized', setLoginWallData);
</script>

        $.trackingParameters = {};
    }
    var contentTracking = {'sent': 1709857032};
    googleTrackingParameters.content = $.extend(googleTrackingParameters.content, contentTracking);
</script>

<script type="text/plain" data-cookieconsent="necessary">
    (function() {
        var addTargetsToAnchors = function() {
            $('#footer-navbar').find('a').each(function() {
                try {
                    var url = new URL($(this).attr('href'));
                    if (url.hostname !== window.location.hostname) {
                        $(this).attr('target', '_blank');
                        return;
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                }
                $(this).attr('target', '_parent');
            });
        }();
    })();
</script>
